<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pandemonium.html>pandemonium</a> (68151)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pandemonium.html>pandemonium</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pandemonium.html>pandemoniums</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pandemonium.html>pandemoniumpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:pandemonium.html>pandemonium</a>, residence of all <a href = vnd.unilang:demons.html>demons</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:devils.html>devils</a>, hell</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:pandemonium.html>pandemonium</a>, a 'hellish' <a href = vnd.unilang:chaos.html>chaos</a>, notably terrible noise and disorder</li></ol>

***pang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a> (12834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The origin of the noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncertain;<sup id="cite_ref-OED_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-OED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possibly derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*pange</i>, perhaps an altered form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">prange</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">prōnge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">affliction, agony, pain; pointed instrument</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as in <i>prongys of deth</i> (“pangs of death, death throes”), from Anglo-<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pronga</i>, of unknown origin. Perhaps connected with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prange</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pranghe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instrument for pinching</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">prang</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse restraint; fetter, neck iron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">prange</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pole, <a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a>; (<i>possibly</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of pillory or stocks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-OED_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-OED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">pyngan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to prick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The word may thus be related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">prong</i>.
</p><p>The verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from the noun.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pangs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A paroxysm of extreme physical pain or anguish; a feeling of sudden and transitory agony; a throe.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1591</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_VI,_Part_2" class="extiw" title="w:Henry VI, Part 2">The Second Part of <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> the Sixt,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="with the Death of the Good Duke Hvmfrey">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene iii], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=RA1-PA137">page 137</a>, column 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><i>War</i>[<i><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></i>]. See how the <b>pangs</b> of death do make him grin. / <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sal.html>Sal</a></i>[<i>isbury</i>]. Diſturbe him not, let him paſſe peaceably.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1601–1602</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twelfth_Night" class="extiw" title="w:Twelfth Night">Twelfe Night, or VVhat You VVill</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene iv], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA269">page 269</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> knight dubb'd with vnhatche'd <a href = vnd.unilang:rapier.html>Rapier</a>, and on carpet conſideration, but he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a diuell in priuate brall, soules and <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> hath he diuorc'd three, and his incenſement at this <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ſo implacable, that ſatisfaction can be none, but by <b>pangs</b> of death and ſepulcher: Hob, nob, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> his word: giu'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> or take'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="ante">a.</abbr></i> <b>1722</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matthew_Prior" class="extiw" title="w:Matthew Prior">Matthew Prior</a>,  “Written in Lady Howe’s Ovid’s Epistles”, in  <cite>The Poetical Works of Matthew Prior, Esq.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title=" | ... |  To which is Prefixed the Life of the Author.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, Edinburgh |  Printed by Mundell and Son,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Royal Bank Close.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1793, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/931361946">931361946</a></small> |  republished in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Anderson_(editor_and_biographer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Anderson (editor and biographer)">Robert Anderson</a>, editor, <cite>The Works of the British <a href = vnd.unilang:poets.html>Poets</a>.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="With Prefaces, Biographical and Critical">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, volume VII, London |  Printed for John amp; Arthur Arch; and for Bell amp; Bradfute, and J. Mundell amp; Co. Edinburgh, 1795, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/221535929">221535929</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=90wwqMPHlHYCamp;pg=PA57-IA456">page 456</a>, column 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But, <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a>! what <b>pangs</b> torment the deſtin’d heart, / That <a href = vnd.unilang:feels.html>feels</a> the wound, yet dare not ſhow the dart; / What eaſe could <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ovid" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ovid">Ovid</a> to his ſorrows give, / Who muſt not ſpeak, and therefore cannot live?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1862</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christina_Rossetti" class="extiw" title="w:Christina Rossetti">Christina <a href = vnd.unilang:rossetti.html>Rossetti</a></a>,  “In the Round Tower at Jhansi, June 8, 1857”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Goblin_Market_and_Other_Poems" class="extiw" title="w:Goblin Market and Other Poems"><a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>Goblin</a> Market and Other Poems</a></cite>, Cambridge; London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macmillan_Publishers" class="extiw" title="w:Macmillan Publishers">Macmillan amp; Co.</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and 23, Henrietta Street, Covent Garden. London.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/36794247">36794247</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=fbdBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA31">page 31</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Will it hurt much?"—"No, mine own: / I wish I could bear the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> for both." / "I wish I could bear the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> alone: / Courage, dear, I am not loth."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1888</b> May,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscar_Wilde" class="extiw" title="w:Oscar Wilde"><a href = vnd.unilang:oscar.html>Oscar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>Wilde</a></a>,  “The <a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>Nightingale</a> and the Rose”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Happy_Prince_and_Other_Tales" class="extiw" title="w:The Happy Prince and Other Tales">The Happy Prince and Other Tales</a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Nutt_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:David Nutt (publisher)">David Nutt</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="270 Strand.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/595167">595167</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/happyprinceother02wild/page/37/mode/1up">pages 37–38</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">So the <a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>Nightingale</a> pressed <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> against the thorn, and the thorn <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> her heart, and a fierce <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> of pain shot through her. Bitter, bitter <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the pain, and <a href = vnd.unilang:wilder.html>wilder</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:wilder.html>wilder</a> grew her song, for she <a href = vnd.unilang:sang.html>sang</a> of the Love that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> perfected by Death, of the Love that <a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a> not in the tomb.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sudden sharp feeling of an emotional or mental nature, as of joy or sorrow.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1843</b> December 19,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="w:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  “Stave Five. The End of It.”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Christmas_Carol" class="extiw" title="w:A Christmas Carol">A Christmas <a href = vnd.unilang:carol.html>Carol</a>. In Prose. Being a Ghost Story of Christmas</a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chapman_%26_Hall" class="extiw" title="w:Chapman amp; Hall">Chapman amp; Hall</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="186, Strand">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/55746801">55746801</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/christmascarolin20dickpage/159/mode/1up">pages 158–159</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> far, when coming on towards him he beheld the portly gentleman, who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> walked into his counting-house the day before, and <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>, "Scrooge and Marley's, I believe?"  It sent a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> across his heart to think how this old gentleman would look upon him when they <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a>; but he <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> what path lay straight before him, and he <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> it.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1867</b> February,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oliver_Wendell_Holmes_Sr." class="extiw" title="w:Oliver Wendell Holmes Sr.">[<a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a> Wendell Holmes Sr.]</a>,  “The Guardian Angel”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Atlantic" class="extiw" title="w:The Atlantic">The Atlantic Monthly. A Magazine of Literature, Art, and Politics</a></cite>, volume XIX, number CXII, Boston, Mass. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ticknor_and_Fields" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ticknor and Fields">Ticknor and Fields</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="124 Tremont Street.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/612185692">612185692</a></small>, chapter VII (<a href = vnd.unilang:myrtle.html>Myrtle</a>’s Letter.—The Young <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a>’s Pursuit.), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=IelIAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA141">page 141</a>, column 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> startled with a piece of information which <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> him such an exquisite <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> of delight that he could hardly keep the usual quiet of his demeanor.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">birth pangs</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a> of conscience</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">pangs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">panging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">panged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cause to have great pain or suffering; to torment, to torture.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1613</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a> |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Fletcher_(playwright)" class="extiw" title="w:John Fletcher (playwright)">[John <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a>]</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_VIII_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Henry VIII (play)">The Famous History of the Life of King <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> the Eight</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act II, scene iii], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=RA1-PA214">page 214</a>, column 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Yet if that quarrell, Fortune, to diuorce / It from the bearer, '<a href = vnd.unilang:tis.html>tis</a> a ſufferance, <b>panging</b> / As ſoule and <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> ſeuering.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1919</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Morley" class="extiw" title="w:Christopher Morley">Christopher Morley</a>,  “On Unanswering Letters”, in  <cite>Mince Pie: Adventures on the Sunny Side of <a href = vnd.unilang:grub.html>Grub</a> Street</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_H._Doran_Company" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George H. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pansa.html>pansa</a> (68146)</h1><br></body> 
***pansy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a> (48725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">pensée</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thought</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as the plant resembles someone that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in deep thought, with a lowered head.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pansies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A cultivated flowering plant, derived by hybridization within species <i><a href = vnd.unilang:viola.html>Viola</a> tricolor</i>.</li>
<li>A deep purple colour, like that of the <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a> colour: <span style="background-color:604E97; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any of various nymphalid butterflies of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Junonia" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Junonia"><i>Junonia</i></a></span>. Also called arguses.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male homosexual, especially one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> effeminate.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A timid, weak <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> or boy; a wuss.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">male homosexual</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">friend of Dorothy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">omi-palone</span>; see also Thesaurus:male homosexual</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">effeminate <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mama.html>mama</a>'s boy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>sissy</a></span>; see also Thesaurus:effeminate <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">timid <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> or boy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mama.html>mama</a>'s boy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nancy.html>nancy</a> boy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>sissy</a></span>; see also Thesaurus:milksop</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Wimpy; spineless; feeble.</li>
<li>Of a deep purple colour, like that of the <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/wild_pansy" class="extiw" title="w:wild pansy">wild <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a></a></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pansified</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pansification</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pensive</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">poise</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">peso</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">panser</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">pantzer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">panciere</i> (whence Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">panchier</i>), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">panse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">panceria</i>. The current spelling and pronunciation <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:panzer.html>Panzer</a></i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantser.html>pantser</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">armour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">car, wagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***papaya.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a> (80544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arawak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Arawak language">Arawak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="arw">papáia</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">papayas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A tropical American evergreen tree, <i>Carica <a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a></i>, having large, yellow, edible fruit</li>
<li>The fruit of this tree.</li>
<li>An orange colour, like that of <a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a> flesh.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a> colour: <span style="background-color:F7A100; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pawpaw</span> (Australia), common term for <a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a>, but strictly speaking this refers to a different tree / fruit</li></ul>
</body>

***papegaai.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:papegaai.html>papegaai</a> (10601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">papegay</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">papegai</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">ببغاء</i> | , of onomatopoeic origin. Cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">popinjay</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papegaai.html>papegaai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papegaaien.html>papegaaien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papegaaitje.html>papegaaitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>parrot, member of the order Psittaciformes, especially of the <a href = vnd.unilang:families.html>families</a> Psittacidae and Psittaculidae</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:parrots.html>parrots</a> other people.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bird-shaped target in archery.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">papist</span></li></ol>

***papier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a> (1971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">papȳrus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πάπυρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pápuros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papieren.html>papieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papiertje.html>papiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> paper (A material used for writing or printing on, made from cellulose pulp rolled into thin sheets.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of paper.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> money (cf. <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> sense of <span class="Latn" lang="en">paper</span>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kladpapier</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">papierbak</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papiermolen.html>papiermolen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">papierwesp</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">toiletpapier</span></li>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pap.html>pap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">porridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zak.html>zak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bag, sack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***paraaf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paraaf.html>paraaf</a> (44880)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">paraphe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paraphus</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">paraph</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paraaf.html>paraaf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parafen.html>parafen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paraaf.html>paraafje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>One's initials used as alternative for an autograph when signing.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">parade</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">parade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:paradijs.html>paradijs</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">paradīs</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paradīsus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράδεισος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parádeisos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Iranian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Iranian language">Proto-Iranian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ira-pro">*paridayjah</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paradijsvogel.html>paradijsvogel</a> (48721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paradijs.html>paradijs</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">paradise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vogel.html>vogel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***paragon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a> (59676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">paragone</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">peragone</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">paragone</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">comparison</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">parangón</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">paragonare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παρακονάω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parakonáō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I sharpen, whet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παρά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pará</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀκόνη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akónē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whetstone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂eḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sharp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">paragons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person of preeminent qualities, who <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> as a pattern or model for others. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">In the novel, <a href = vnd.unilang:constanza.html>Constanza</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></b> of virtue who would never compromise her reputation.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1599–1602</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hamlet" class="extiw" title="w:Hamlet">The <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>Tragedie</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a>, Prince of Denmarke</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. </p>
<ol><li>To compare; to parallel; to put in rivalry or emulation with.

<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1603–1604</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Othello" class="extiw" title="w:Othello">The <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>Tragedie</a> of Othello, the Moore of Venice</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">paragraphe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paragraphus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sign for start of a new section of discourse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράγραφος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parágraphos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παρά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pará</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beside</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γράφω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gráphō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***paranoia.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paranoia.html>paranoia</a> (11015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράνοια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paránoia</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">madness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">psychology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paranoia.html>paranoia</a></span></li></ol>

***parasiet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasiet</a> (12279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">parasite</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">parasitus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράσιτος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parásitos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 16th century. The sense “parasitic organism” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic loan</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">parasite</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasiet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasieten.html>parasieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parasite <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">parasitic organism</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:luizen.html>Luizen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vlooien.html>vlooien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vampiers.html>vampiers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> bloedergerlijke <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parasieten.html>parasieten</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>Lice, flees and other vampires are bloody annoying <b>parasites</b>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parasite, someone who relies on others to get <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> done. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tafelschuimer</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">wondparasiet</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">zwakteparasiet</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasitair.html>parasitair</a></span></li>

***parel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parel.html>parel</a> (11244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">perle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">peerle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">paerle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:parle.html>parle</a></i>, presumably <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">perle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">perla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perla</i>, plausibly a diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clam, pearl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pearl</i>; alternative derivations from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">birna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">beryllus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beryl.html>beryl</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> lack plausibility; the letter sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> apparently popular etymology from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">nonparel</i>, itself from French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">nonpareille</i>. Its typographic use <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">perle</i>, following the name given by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean_Jannon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jean Jannon">Jean Jannon</a> to the type used in his miniature editions of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vergil" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vergil">Vergil</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horace" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Horace">Horace</a>, amp; the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Testament" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:New Testament">New <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a></a> in the 1620s, which <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the smallest printed works to his time.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parel.html>parel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parels.html>parels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parelen.html>parelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pareltje.html>pareltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pearl, a precious, round <a href = vnd.unilang:shelly.html>shelly</a> concretion from oysters or other molluscs</li>
<li>Its imitation</li>
<li>Mother of pearl, the natural material pearls are made from</li>
<li>Anything resembling a pearl's irregular ball-shape, notably a drop of liquid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (One of) the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> quality, first pick, the cream</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The size of type between <a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a> and nonparel, equated with the English pearl and standardized as 5 point.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">5-point type</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parisienne.html>parisienne</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parelen.html>parelen</a></span></li>

***parfum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a> (4471)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">parfumer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfums.html>parfums</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfumpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A perfume, a luxury product providing a fragrant scent.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Essence <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rozen.html>rozen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> diverse <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloemen.html>bloemen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geren.html>gegeerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:natuurlijke.html>natuurlijke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parfums.html>parfums</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Essence of roses and various others flowers <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in high demand for natural <b>perfumes</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">reukwerk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">parfument</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A perfume, a pleasant scent.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roos.html>roos</a> Friesia <a href = vnd.unilang:verspreidt.html>verspreidt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemels.html>hemels</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> Friesia gives out a heavenly <b>scent</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
